000000r 1               ;SquatM beeper music engine
000000r 1               ;Originally written by Shiru 06'17 for ZX Spectrum 48K
000000r 1               ;Ported to Atari 8-bit by Shiru 07'21
000000r 1               ;Ported to the Acorn Electron by Negative Charge 11'22
000000r 1               
000000r 1               SHEILA_COUNTER          = $FE06
000000r 1               SHEILA_MISC_CONTROL     = $FE07
000000r 1               OSBYTE                  = $FFF4
000000r 1

000000r 1               OP_ROL_A 				= $2A

00002Br 1  20 F4 FF     	JSR     OSBYTE                                          ; Old value returned in X

000030r 1  8A           	TXA
000031r 1  29 F8        	AND     #$F8                                            ; Mask - 11111000
000033r 1  85 rr        	STA     speaker_off                                     ; Store previous FE07 values for CAPS LOCK LED, CASSETTE MOTOR, and DISPLAY MODE
000035r 1  09 02        	ORA     #$02                                            ; Switch on sound generation - 00000010
000037r 1  85 rr        	STA     speaker_on                                      ; Store previous FE07 value with sound generation enabled
000039r 1  A9 00        	LDA     #$00
00003Br 1  8D 06 FE     	STA     SHEILA_COUNTER                                  ; Zero the ULA SHEILA counter (FE06), creating a toggle speaker (inaudible frequency)
00003Er 1  A2 00        	LDX     #$00                                            ; Clear X
